31/10/2015, 5:03 pm - DineshKarthik Raveendran: My open letter on┬атАк#тАОDeepawali_DiwaliтАм. Pls spare a minute to read :
Now-a-days I am observing people sharing posts saying "No crackers this Diwali, save environment." Well, I appreciate their concern, but I ask why we are indirectly depleting ozone layer by daily AC usage? Why we use Deos and refrigerators very commonly which generates chloro-flouro carbons which harm environment? I too studied science!
Let me share some facts I understood from Indian rituals and science behind them, every festival here has some relation to do with nature's well being which includes Human beings too.
Deepawali or Diwali is a festival of lights celebrated in a period when atmosphere contains less heat, which implies in more increase of micro organisms and their quick spreading.
We light diy─Бs(Deepams) in this festival to generate heat in environment which destroys ill spreading organisms. And fire crackers. We used to write an essay about Diwali in Hindi exam, but with a pride in celebrating the festival.
Dear people who think you are doing much good to nature by spreading the message to stop Festivals, I ask you to know and spread the message ofтАк#тАОEarthDayтАм, I ask you to plant a tree atleast yearly and show your love to nature.
There is an industry of fire works who work all over the year and their fate gets decided in just less than a month from now. Now I ask you to sit against the government which says Tobacco is injurious to health in cinema theatres and give licenses for shops to sell Tobacco. We all laugh at mukesh ad. Right??
I love environment, bcoz it is motherly form for all beings. But for your information, nature needs some heat when it cannot create heat by itself.
Have some understanding about Festivals of homeland! Have some support for motherland.
Some say Diwali is a festival of loud sounds which may harm humans and animals. I ask them "Do you think and believe that every activity you daily do for your well-being is conscious? Are we even sure that the food you are eating outside is safe?"
Not like loud parties we love to dance for some meaningless beat.
Just a festival with a reason celebrated on a day of every year, and we love to celebrate it proudly.
Let us celebrate.
Happy Deep─Бwali in advance! Many lights in our lives!
тАк#тАОJaiHindтАм

04/12/2015, 10:11 am - Prakash Web 2. 0: #ChennaiRainsHelp 

Routes Update :
Kanchipuram to Koyembedu: the road is quite good. There are areas that have potholes, but no water logging at all.
2. Maduravoil flyover: you cannot head towards Tambaram, so avoid the flyover completely.
3. Koyembedu flyover to Chetpet Bridge: Absolutely no problem on the roads.
4. Chetpet Bridge to Gemini: again, no problem, except for a bit of water logging on Nungambakkam High Road.
5. Gemini to TTK Road signal: no problem.
6. TTK Road signal to RA Puram: no problem, but a bit of water logging near Billroth Hospital.
7. DO NOT HEAD TOWARDS KOTTURPURAM BRIDGE, AS IT HAS BEEN CLOSED. There is significant water logging on the stretch from Greenways Road signal to Boat Club area.
8. Billroth Hospital signal to Music College via Mylapore: no problem except for a bit of water logging near the playground next to Music College.
9. Adyar Bridge: no problem, but the Adyar Flyover is closed.
10. Adyar signal to Thiruvanmiyur signal: no problem.
11. THIS IS THE PROBLEM AREA: heavy water logging towards Buckingham Canal AND towards Tidel Park SIGNAL (basically the only 2 options to reach the OMR). I opted for the Tidel Park signal and almost got stuck in the water.
12. If you safely cross to the OMR, the road is motorable up to the Perungudi toll plaza.
